        SELECT 1
        FROM [Product_image] AS [p]
        WHERE [m].[Product_id] = [p].[Product_id]) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)

    WHEN EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM [Product_image] AS [p]
        WHERE [m].[Product_id] = [p].[Product_id]) THEN CAST(1 AS bit)
    ELSE CAST(0 AS bit)
END, [t0].[Product_image_id], [t0].[Product_id], [t0].[Product_image]
FROM [Menu] AS [m]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [t].[Product_image_id], [t].[Product_id], [t].[Product_image]
    FROM (
        SELECT [p0].[Product_image_id], [p0].[Product_id], [p0].[Product_image], ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY [p0].[Product_id] ORDER BY [p0].[Product_image_id]) AS [row]
        FROM [Product_image] AS [p0]
    ) AS [t]
    WHERE [t].[row] <= 1
) AS [t0] ON [m].[Product_id] = [t0].[Product_id]
WHERE ([m].[IsDelete] = CAST(0 AS bit)) OR ([m].[IsDelete] IS NULL)
ORDER BY [m].[Product_name]
